About this document

Proteus 2000 stuff.

Related to all the Proteus 2000 family synthesizers from E-mu and Ensoniq.

Banks and Programs

Bank Selects and Program Changes.

Synths and Banks

Proteus 2000
Composer
04 cmpsr: CMPSR
Halo
Sounds of the ZR
08 qrom: QROM = HALO = ZR76 = ZR-76
XK-6
X-Lead V2
14 xrom: XROM = XROM1 (???)
Proteus 2500
Proteus Pop Collection
17 p2500: P2500 = 2500 (???)
Orbit 3
Techno Synth Construction Yard
65 tecno: TeCnO
Beat Garden
67 beat: BEAT

E-mu ROMs

(The counts are: banks presets / instruments / arps / riffs)

      abbreviated name
      --------------------
  id  my     rom    manual   prodatum    full name - comments
  --  -----  -----  ------   ----------  -------------------------------------
 *00* user   USER   USER     User        User
                                           - counts: 4 512 / 0 / ? / ?
  02  ...    ...    ...      XTREM       ...
  03  ...    ...    ...      Audity      ...

                                           - synth: Proteus 2000
                                           - same wave instruments as 17 p2500
                                           - counts: 8 1024 / 1173 / 0 / 388
  05  ...    ...    ...      Protozoa    Protozoa
  06  ...    ...    ...      B3          Definitive B-3
  07  ...    ...    ...      XL-1        X-Lead V1
                                           - counts: 4? 511? / 1209? / ? / ?

                                           - synth: Ensoniq Halo
                                           - my abbrev: "halo" or "qrom"?
                                           - counts: 5 639 / 443 / 299 / 640
  09  ...    ...    WORLD    World Exp.  World Expedition
                                           - synth: Planet Earth
  10  ...    ...    ORCH1    Orch 1      Orchestral Sessions Volume 1
                                           - synth: Virtuoso 2000
                                           - counts: 3? 383? / 81? / ? / ?
  11  ...    ...    ORCH2    Orch 2      Orchestral Sessions Volume 2
                                           - synth: Virtuoso 2000
                                           - counts: 2? 255? / 240? / ? / ?
  13  ...    ...    ...      Mo'Phatt    ...
 *14* xrom   XROM   XROM1    XL-2        X-Lead V2
                                           - synth: XK-6
                                           - counts: 5 639 / 1209 / ? / ?
                                           - the XK-6 manual says this rom is
                                             id:07 XROM1
  15   = 13                              ...
  16  ...    ...    ...      Ensoniq     Ensoniq Project
 *17* p2500  P2500  P2500    PROM1       Proteus Pop Collection
                                           - synth: Proteus 2500
                                           - synth: PK-6
                                           - manual also calls it "2500"
                                           - same wave instruments as 04 cmpsr
                                           - counts: 4 511 / 1173 / 299 / 500

  19  ...    ...    DRUM     DRUM        Protean Drum

  64  ...    ...    ...      Holy Grail  The Holy Grail Piano (?)

Banks and Programs (Presets)

             dec               hex
             --------------    --------------
  Bank       msb lsb  prg      msb lsb  prg      First preset in bank
  -------    --- ---  -----    --- ---  -----    ----------------------
  user-0       0   0  0-127     00  00  00-7F
  user-1       0   1  0-127     00  01  00-7F
  user-2       0   2  0-127     00  02  00-7F
  user-3       0   3  0-127     00  03  00-7F

  cmpsr-0      4   0  0-127     04  00  00-7F    000. brs: SforzadoSect
  cmpsr-1      4   1  0-127     04  01  00-7F    000. wav: CZ101 Digi
  cmpsr-2      4   2  0-127     04  02  00-7F    000. pad: MetalBeats
  cmpsr-3      4   3  0-127     04  03  00-7F    000. prc: Acidphone
  cmpsr-4      4   4  0-127     04  04  00-7F    000. kb1: DynamicGrand
  cmpsr-5      4   5  0-127     04  05  00-7F    000. kb4: Dance
  cmpsr-6      4   6  0-127     04  06  00-7F    000. bs3: Sub-Basement
  cmpsr-7      4   7  0-127     04  07  00-7F    000. bs5: Ultimate 2

  qrom-0       8   0  0-127     08  00  00-7F    000. kb1: PerfectPno 1
  qrom-1       8   1  0-127     08  01  00-7F    000. kb1: Piano 1-GM
  qrom-2       8   2  0-127     08  02  00-7F    000. syn: Bella
  qrom-3       8   3  0-127     08  03  00-7F    000. kit: Live
  qrom-4       8   4  0-127     08  04  00-7F    000. jam: Grand Piano

  xrom-0      14   0  0-127     0E  00  00-7F    000. kit: K-0
  xrom-1      14   1  0-127     0E  01  00-7F    000. syn: Basic Saw
  xrom-2      14   2  0-127     0E  02  00-7F    000. bas: Top Tri
  xrom-3      14   3  0-127     0E  03  00-7F    000. arp: Deeper Love
  xrom-4      14   4  0-127     0E  04  00-7F    000. jam: Gothica

  p2500-0     17   0  0-127     11  00  00-7F    000. arp: Guitartar
  p2500-1     17   1  0-127     11  01  00-7F    000. kit: Acoustic 1&2
  p2500-2     17   2  0-127     11  02  00-7F    000. led: Wormy
  p2500-3     17   3  0-127     11  03  00-7F    000. pad: Richness

  tecno-0     65   0  0-127     41  00  00-7F    000. hit: Intruder
  tecno-1     65   1  0-127     41  01  00-7F    000. bas: To B@SS 2
  tecno-2     65   2  0-127     41  02  00-7F    000. kit: TeCnO 2
  tecno-3     65   3  0-127     41  03  00-7F    000. arp: Dutch Dance

  beat-0      67   0  0-127     43  00  00-7F    000. bts: Beat Garden
  beat-1      67   1  0-127     43  01  00-7F    000. pr1: Cajon
  beat-2      67   2  0-127     43  02  00-7F    000. sfx: a cold wind
  beat-3      67   3  0-127     43  03  00-7F    000. bas: Marc One

  multi-0     80   0  0-63      50  00  00-3F    000. User Setup

MIDI messages and bytes:

          Midi Message               dec               hex         hex
          -----------------------    --------------    --------    -----------
  msb:    Control Change  0 = 00h    176-191  0 vvv    Bn 00 vv    B0-BF 00 vv
  lsb:    Control Change 32 = 20h    176-191 32 vvv    Bn 20 vv    B0-BF 20 vv
  prg:    Program Change             192-207    vvv    Cn    vv    C0-CF    vv

Instruments

Instrument categories

Halo

Alphabetic order:

  bas:  ? Bass [???]
  brs: Brass Instrument
  epo: Electric Piano
  gtr: Guitar
  hit:  ? Hit [???]
  kit: Drum Kit
  nse:  ? Noise [???]
  org:  ? Organ [???]
  pno:  ? Piano [???]
  prc: Percussion
  sfx: Sound Effects
  str: String, Violin, Cello, etc.
  syn: Synthesizer
  vox: Vocal Sound
  wav:  ? Wave [???]
  wnd: Wind Instrument

Order used in the instrument list:

  pno:  ? Piano [???]
  epo: Electric Piano
  org:  ? Organ [???]
  bas:  ? Bass [???]
  gtr: Guitar
  str: String, Violin, Cello, etc.
  brs: Brass Instrument
  wnd: Wind Instrument
  vox: Vocal Sound
  wav:  ? Wave [???]
  syn: Synthesizer
  hit:  ? Hit [???]
  sfx: Sound Effects
  nse:  ? Noise [???]
  prc: Percussion
  kit: Drum Kit
  prc: Percussion [again]

Presets

Halo: Relationship between ROM presets and user presets

Different names for the ROM preset bank:

  HALO  - from the Halo manual
  QROM  - from the Halo I bought
  ZR-76 - from Prodatum

Below, I'm using the lower case version of these.

User and ROM preset banks from the Halo manual:

  user-0  =  halo-4  -  000. jam: Grand Piano
  user-1  =  halo-0  -  000. kb1: PerfectPno 1
  user-2  =  halo-1  -  000. kb1: Piano 1-GM
  user-3  =  halo-2  -  000. syn: Bella
             halo-3  -  000. kit: Live

User and ROM preset banks from the Halo synth I bought:

  user-0  =  qrom-4  -  000. jam: Grand Piano
  user-1  =  qrom-0  -  000. kb1: PerfectPno 1
  user-2  =  qrom-2  -  000. syn: Bella
  user-3  =  qrom-3  -  000. kit: Live
             qrom-1  -  000. kb1: Piano 1-GM

ROM and User preset banks:

  HALO  /  QROM       Manual     Synth      First preset in bank
  ---------------     ------     ------     ----------------------
  halo-0 = qrom-0  =  user-1  =  user-1  -  000. kb1: PerfectPno 1
  halo-1 = qrom-1  =  user-2  =          -  000. kb1: Piano 1-GM
  halo-2 = qrom-2  =  user-3  =  user-2  -  000. syn: Bella
  halo-3 = qrom-3  =          =  user-3  -  000. kit: Live
  halo-4 = qrom-4  =  user-0  =  user-0  -  000. jam: Grand Piano

Halo Preset categories

From the manual:

  arp: Arpeggiated
  brs: Brass Instrument
  bpm: Synchro-sonic, rythmic
  bs1: Bass 1, Acoustic Bass
  bs2: Bass 2, Bass Guitar
  bs3: Bass 3, Synth Bass
  bts: Beats presets
  gtr: Guitar
  kb1: Keyboard 1, Piano
  kb2: Keyboard 2, Electric Piano
  kb3: Keyboard 3, Organ
  jam: Press Audition & play along
  key: Keyboard instrument, organ
  kit: Drum Kit
  led: Lead Instrument
  orc: Orchestral Instrument
  pad: Sustained, full
  prc: Percussion
  sfx: Sound Effects
  str: String, Violin, Cello, etc.
  syn: Synthesizer
  vox: Vocal Sound
  wnd: Wind Instrument

From the manual and from the instrument list:

  arp: Arpeggiated
  bpm: Synchro-sonic, rythmic
  brs: Brass Instrument

MIDI

Controller Knobs

The typical patching of the controller knobs

(From my Proteus 2500 synth and the Proteus 2500 Manual, "Front Panel Knob Functions", page 287-288)

     Name           Patching / Function
     -------------  -----------------------------------------------
  A  Filter Cutoff  Filter Frequency
  B  Filter Q       Filter Resonance
  C  Filter Attack  Filter Envelope Attack Rate
  D  Filter Decay   Filter Envelope Decay and Release Rate

  E  Amp Attack     Volume Envelope Attack Rate
  F  Amp Decay      Volume Envelope Decay Rate
  G  Amp Sustain    Volume Envelope Sustain Level
  H  Amp Release    Volume Envelope Release Rate

  I  Vel -> Amp     Key Velocity to Volume
  J  Vel -> Filter  Key Velocity to Filter Frequency
  K  LFO2 Amount    LFO 2 Amount
  L  LFO2 Rate      LFO 2 Frequency

  M  Mod 1          Alternate Modulation Parameter 1
  N  Mod 2          Alternate Modulation Parameter 2
  O  Arp Velocity   Scales the Velocity values of arpeggiated notes
  P  Arp Gate       Varies the arpeggiator Gate Time

The names above are from the synth [XXX: Check this]. The manual differs for the following four:

     Name                Patching / Function
     ------------------  -----------------------------------------------
  I  Velocity -> Amp     Key Velocity to Volume
  J  Velocity -> Filter  Key Velocity to Filter Frequency
  K  LFO 2 Amount        LFO 2 Amount
  L  LFO 2 Rate          LFO 2 Frequency

(From the Halo Manual, "Front Panel Knob Functions", page 210-209)

     Name       Patching / Function
     ---------  -----------------------------------------------------
  A  Tone       Filter Frequency
  B  Presence   Filter Resonance
  C  Shape      Volume/Filter Envelope Amount(?) (manual says Attack)
  D  Image      Pitch / Glide / Chorus Amount / Layer Volume

  E  Attack     Volume/Filter Envelope Attack
  F  Decay/Rls  Volume/Filter Envelope Decay/Release
  G  Movement   LFO -> Dynamic Movement (for example Panning)
  H  Rate       LFO Rate

  I  Dynamic 1  Typically Velocity -> Amplifier Volume
  J  Dynamic 2  Typically Velocity -> Filter Frequency
  K  Dynamic 3  Effects Processor A Amount
  L  Dynamic 4  Effects Processor B Amount

The default assignment of controller knobs from/to MIDI control numbers

(From my Proteus 2500 synth and the Proteus 2500 Manual, "Real-time Controller Assignment", page 121)

                   MIDI Control
     Name          dec hex  Description
     ------------- --- ---  ---------------------------------------------------
  A  Filter Cutoff  74  4A  Sound Controller 5 (def: Brightness)
  B  Filter Q       71  47  Sound Controller 2 (def: Timbre/Harmonic Intensity)
  C  Filter Attack  25  19  Undefined
  D  Filter Decay   26  1A  Undefined

  E  Amp Attack     73  49  Sound Controller 4 (def: Attack Time)
  F  Amp Decay      75  4B  Undefined
  G  Amp Sustain    85  55  Undefined
  H  Amp Release    72  48  Sound Controller 3 (def: Release Time)

  I  Vel -> Amp     78  4E  Sound Controller 9 (def: Vibrato Delay)
  J  Vel -> Filter  77  4D  Sound Controller 8 (def: Vibrato Depth)
  K  LFO2 Amount    27  1B  Undefined
  L  LFO2 Rate      28  1C  Undefined

  M  Mod 1          91  5B  Effects 1 Depth (def: Reverb Send Level)
  N  Mod 2          93  5D  Effects 3 Depth (def: Chorus Send Level)
  O  Arp Velocity   82  52  General Purpose Controllers 7
  P  Arp Gate       83  53  General Purpose Controllers 8

[XXX: Check Midi-M and Midi-N on the Proteus 2500 synth]

The settings for MIDI controller M and N above are actually taken from my Halo synth, not the Halo manual. The settings in the manual and the synth match for all settings, except for controllers M and N, where the manual says:

  M             01  01  Modulation Wheel or Lever
  N             03  03  Undefined

MIDI SysEx

Halo: Pitch wheel flutter

My Halo randomly sends the following pitch wheel MIDI bytes fluttering now and then:

  E0 40 44
  E0 00 43

So when doing sysex dumps the MIDI setting "Keyboard outputs MIDI" should be set to "don't transmit".

Dumping MIDI sysex data from Halo to Linux

When dumping MIDI sysex from Halo to Linux, the MIDI setting "MIDI sysex packet delay" can actually be kept at 0 milliseconds. But to see what's happening when dumping banks it should be set to 25 milliseconds.

Here's one way to dump MIDI sysex from Halo to Linux:

  $ amidi -p $port -t $timeout -r $file

For example:

  $ time amidi -p hw:1,0,0 -t 2 -r bank-user-0.syx

  206720 bytes read

  real    1m18.676s
  user    0m0.148s
  sys     0m2.360s

Sending MIDI sysex data from Linux to Halo

When sending MIDI sysex back from Linux to Halo, the following amidi command can be used for most data:

  $ amidi -p $port -s $file

For example:

  $ amidi -p hw:1,0,0 -s all-user-arp-patterns.syx

The only exception is sending banks, which results in an error message [XXX]. These need a delay. I couldn't find any midi sysex tools which could do this, so I took the "slowcat" script from the Perl Cookbook, changed it slightly and renamed it to "sleepycat". Here's how to use it:

  $ sleepycat -$delay $file > $mididevice

For example:

  $ time sleepycat -0.0004 bank-user-0.syx > /dev/midi1

  real    1m??.???s  # [XXX check the typical time]
  user    ?m?.???s
  sys     ?m?.???s

A delay of 0.0004 seconds seems to work OK, while delays of 0.0003 seconds and shorter gives the error.

Here's the "sleepycat" script:

  #!/usr/bin/perl
  # sleepycat
  # based on slowcat from the perl cookbook
  # slowcat - emulate a   s l o w   line printer
  # usage: slowcat [-DELAY] [files ...]

  use Time::HiRes;

  $Delay = ($ARGV[0] =~ /^-([.\d]+)/) ? (shift, $1) : 0.001;
  $| = 1;

  while (<>) {
      for (split(//)) {
          print;
          #select(undef,undef,undef, 0.005 * $Delay);
          Time::HiRes::sleep($Delay);
      }
  }

Miscellaneous

Linux command line

Changing the device number of all SysEx files

Make sure to set $d to the correct destination directory.

  $ (d="somedir"; for f in *.syx; do :; echo $f; halo-change-device-id -0 < $f > ../$d/$f; done)

Listing the first line of all MIDI SysEx dumps

  $ (for f in *.syx; do :; echo "--- $f"; xxd -g1 < $f | head -n1; done) | dye '(?<=f0 18 0f )(..)' ir 'f0 18 0f' ig '^--- .*' ib

Show the difference between two SysEx dumps (the whole file)

  $ wdiff -t <( xxd -g1 < $file1 ) <( xxd -g1 < $file2 ) | less -r

Show the difference between two SysEx dumps (only differing lines)

  $ diff -u0 <( xxd -g1 < $file1 ) <( xxd -g1 < $file2 ) | wdiff -dt | less -r

The Proteus 2000 Program Change script

  $ p2kpc -?  # = proteus-2000-program-change --help
  Proteus 2000 Program Change v0.02 2010-10-21 Erik Warendorph
  Usage:  p2kpc [options] [channel] <bank_msb>-<bank_lsb>-<preset>
  or use it as a filter with each input line matching:
    [channel] <bank_msb>-<bank_lsb>-<preset>
  Options:
    -v  --verbose            Be verbose
    -?  --help               Display this help and exit
  The channel defaults to 1.  The dashes between bank_msb, bank_lsb and preset
  can (currently) be substituted with spaces (but this might change later).
  The following bank_msb names may be used instead of the bank_msb:
    00 = user
    04 = cmpsr
    08 = qrom
    17 = p2500
    65 = tecno
    67 = beat
    80 = multi
  (There are also other bank_msb name aliases (see source), but they might
  change later.  So they are OK on the command line, but should be avoided in
  scripts.)
  Vim usage:                            (Don't include these descriptions)
    :sil .w !p2kpc                      Execute for current line
    @:                                  Repeat on another line
    :map <F12> :sil .w !p2kpc<Enter>    Make a mapping

Changing the device id, the bank and preset numbers and other SysEx values
